After discussing and formulating a plan, the results of the meeting will be telegraphed to the government for reference.

Shanghai Bar Association Declaration

Extradition of Political Prisoners Violates the General Principles of International Law

Careful Attention Should Be Paid to Laws and Agreements

The Shanghai Bar Association issued a declaration yesterday stating that on April 30th of this year, detectives from the French Concession police, along with Japanese military police, went to 27 Baokang Lane, Avenue Joffre, to arrest Korean Li Chunshan. At that time, Li was out, and Ahn Chang-ho, who became a Chinese citizen in 1922, happened to be there and was detained. He was taken to the Louza Police Station along with 25 other Koreans who were arrested at the same time and sent to the Japanese military camp. Since this incident, due to criticisms from Chinese and foreign newspapers, the French Concession authorities issued a statement in Chinese and Western languages on the 13th of this month, defending their actions as legal. However, based on the facts recorded by various parties, the following four points were not clarified in the statement: (1) Ahn Chang-ho's arrest was without a warrant and was the result of being accidentally found at Li Chunshan's residence; (2) Ahn Chang-ho's Chinese nationality; (3) The location to which the arrested persons were taken was either the Japanese consular court or the Japanese military camp; (4) The similar provisions in Chinese and foreign laws regarding political prisoners, which have been the custom of the Concession for decades. That is, unless a crime is in progress, the police must obtain a warrant from the judicial authorities before making an arrest. If Ahn Chang-ho was arrested on that day because he happened to visit Li Chunshan's house and was encountered by the Japanese military police, and the arrest was made without a prior warrant, then it is a well-known fact that the actions of the French Concession police violated the legal provisions protecting the freedom of the people and the customs of the Concession. The impact on the future of the people of the French Concession is self-evident. Secondly, regarding the issue of Ahn Chang-ho's nationality, it is an undeniable fact that Ahn Chang-ho has Chinese nationality. The French Concession authorities' statement that the arrested persons claimed to be Korean nationals refers to their failure to renounce their original Japanese nationality. In the event of dual nationality, the principles of international law should be applied, and the law of the country where the person is located should be followed. Chinese law stipulates that anyone naturalized as a Chinese citizen with the permission of the government is a Chinese citizen and does not require formal renunciation of their original nationality. Therefore, Koreans who have obtained Chinese nationality, even if they have not renounced Japanese nationality, should be regarded as Chinese citizens within Chinese territory. The French Concession police, without obtaining a warrant from the court, arrested him and did not send him to court within 24 hours, but sent this Chinese citizen to the Japanese military camp, which was in conflict with China. What is the impact of this action on Chinese sovereignty and the stimulation of the Chinese people? The statement also stated that, according to current treaties, countries that have jurisdiction over their nationals in China can execute warrants issued by their judicial authorities within the Concessions. We have not heard of whether this treaty has been agreed to by the Chinese government, and it is even more unknown. Even if this treaty is considered valid, its scope is limited to purely judicial matters, and the Concession police are only obligated to execute it. Whether the current arrest of Koreans was ordered by a Japanese judicial officer or requested by the Japanese military police is unknown. However, after being taken to the Japanese side, according to newspaper reports, the arrested persons were imprisoned in a Japanese military camp, which clearly shows that the arrest was not initiated by the judiciary but by the military. The Concession police may have the responsibility to execute the orders of the judicial authorities of various countries with extraterritorial rights, but they cannot be said to have the responsibility to execute the orders of the military of various countries. This is what the statement failed to explain to us. Furthermore, it is a well-known fact that the Koreans whom the Japanese authorities requested the French Concession to arrest this time were all political prisoners. According to the general principles of international law, political prisoners residing in other countries should be protected by the host country and should not be extradited. France, in particular, is a country that is happy to protect political prisoners. The recent case of Koutiepov, in which the Paris police spared no effort in investigating it, is a clear example. The Korean people fled to the French Concession in Shanghai seeking independence for their country. They have a special responsibility to protect these political prisoners. Now, at the request of the Japanese authorities, they were all arrested and sent to the Japanese military camp. This is a move that greatly violates international law, and no one can defend it. In a French Concession with such a dense population, the maintenance of order and the prosperity of the market depend on the strict adherence to the law by the judicial and police organs. If residents can be arbitrarily arrested and punished, and the Sino-French agreement can be disregarded at will, then the people's property, security, and freedom will be lost. Such a large Chinese and foreign commercial center will fall into a dangerous state without laws, and its future will inevitably lead to unimaginable circumstances. Moreover, it will make the Chinese people doubt France's diplomatic policy towards China, believing that it may be biased and lead to such actions. In order to strive for the security of the residents of the French Concession, and to prevent misunderstandings between the Chinese and French people, which may affect the close relations between the two countries for decades, we hope that the French Concession authorities will pay careful attention to the law and agreements in handling any event, so as not to repeat the mistakes of this time. It must be understood that the law is the only guarantee of the people. If the law is disregarded, then society will not be able to continue to exist, and those who bear this responsibility are especially the local administrative organs. The Concession authorities should not ignore this important responsibility. Shanghai Bar Association, May 17, 1932.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Request for Protest Against the Arrest of Ahn Chang-ho

Should be Handed Back and Tried by Our Courts

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday regarding the French Concession's handing over of Ahn Chang-ho to the Japanese, requesting that they protest and insist that our country conduct the trial itself. The telegram reads: "To the Executive Yuan in Luoyang, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing: Ahn Chang-ho, a Korean arrested by the Japanese in the French Concession in connection with the Hongkou bomb incident, has been found to have been naturalized as a Chinese citizen. The archives of the former Ministry of Interior and the government gazettes can be consulted. The Shanghai Bar Association is also reported to have sent a separate telegram clarifying this matter. According to the international principles of non-extradition of political prisoners and non-extradition of nationals, our country cannot allow the Japanese to arrest him freely. In order to comply with the agreement on the recovery of the Mixed Court, the French authorities should not have allowed the Japanese side to arrest and hand over our nationals without trial by the Chinese courts. It is heard that the French consul later excused himself, saying that Ahn Chang-ho did not declare himself to be Chinese at the time, and there was no supporting evidence, which is difficult to believe and is certainly not reasonable. The Japanese have brazenly taken Ahn Chang-ho to their country without any regard. If our government tolerates this, not only will our legal rights be infringed upon, but it will also make small and weak nations feel disheartened. It is proposed that your esteemed Yuan and Ministry make a serious protest to the French and Japanese ambassadors, ordering them to return Ahn Chang-ho. Whether he is involved in the bomb incident should be investigated and handled by our courts to avoid setting a bad precedent in international law and causing criticism from both China and foreign countries. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

Chen Mingshu and Chen Gongbo

Leave Shanghai for Nanjing One After the Other

Fundraising for the Ministry of Industry Shows Promise

Minister of Communications Chen Mingshu and Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo left Shanghai for Nanjing in the early mornings of the past two days after their previous visit to Shanghai. Minister of Communications Chen Mingshu stayed in Shanghai for about a week. Before going to Hangzhou (the 10th), he once visited and spoke with Mr. Sun Zhesheng. It is heard that Sun only stated that the program for resisting Japan and saving the country that he proposed was merely a contribution of opinions to the central government, and that the drafting of this program was entirely based on the conversations and opinions exchanged with President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei during his visit to Shanghai. As for the rumors of meetings in Hangzhou, those close to Sun said that this matter has now become a thing of the past. Sun had this intention when publishing the program for resisting Japan and saving the country, but he has now completely abandoned it. Although Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo did not specifically visit Sun, they did meet once. Chen's visit to Shanghai was not solely for the purpose of visiting Sun. His main task, it is heard, was to raise funds from the industrial sector, and it is also heard that after contact with the industrial sector, there has been some progress. Various Trade Associations Telegraph the National Government

Reiterating the Request to Recover Lost Territories

The various trade associations in the city telegraphed the National Government in Luoyang yesterday, saying: "To the National Government in Luoyang: The Northeast has been lost for half a decade. Our patriotic self-defense volunteer armies have been fighting bitterly in the White Mountains and Black Waters. As one falls, another rises, becoming more and more fierce. If the authorities provide financial and material support and unified command, then there would be no puppet regime in Southern Mongolia long ago. Not doing so has allowed the puppet regime to grow larger and stronger, forming a situation where it is too late to stop it from becoming a snake. Now that the invading Japanese soldiers in Shanghai have been transferred north, the atmosphere at the customs has suddenly become tense. The volunteer armies in the Northeast are fearful of the morning dew, and the provinces of Hebei and Shandong feel even more at risk. This is exactly what the Grand Master Jia called the time to cry bitterly and sigh deeply. Looking around the country, the military clamor in Guangzhou and the scholastic debates in Taishan have not forgotten the struggle for petty gains, as if they do not know that there is a national crisis at hand. Alas, the bronze camel will meet you in the thorns! It is necessary to mend the fold after losing the sheep, and it is not too late to take action at sunset. At this time, when the hearts of the people in the Northeast have not completely died, and the Japanese troops have not yet concentrated, we still hope that you will quickly mobilize the elite troops in the Southeast, order the generals to go out of the pass, drive out the ugly captives, and return our mountains and rivers. You will see that the compatriots in the Northeast will rejoice at the restoration of the Han palace rituals, and will welcome the teachers with pots of rice soup. The people in the rear will also be fortunate that the descendants of the gods and emperors have not perished, and will destroy their homes to relieve the national crisis. Then the invaders will not be enough to pacify, and the shame will not be difficult to erase. The continuation of the country's destiny and the survival of the nation depend on this one move. Please do not regard it as fodder and treat it lightly. The Shanghai Cotton Cloth Industry Trade Association, the Color Printing Industry Trade Association, the Shanghai Sales of Lime Trade Association, the Shanghai Mineral Ash Factory Trade Association, the Sugar Industry Trade Association, the Intestine Industry Trade Association, the Brick and Ash Industry Trade Association, the Ramie Bag Industry Trade Association, the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Trade Association, the Paper Industry Trade Association, the Silk and Satin Industry Trade Association, the Yarn Industry Trade Association, the Waste Cotton Industry Trade Association, the Ginseng and Bird's Nest Industry Trade Association, and the Electrical Appliance Industry Trade Association respectfully."

Northeast Fellow-Villagers Association Asks for Aid to the Volunteer Armies

Tea Party to be Convened This Afternoon

The Northeast Fellow-Villagers Association in Shanghai issued a public notice requesting all sectors to aid the Northeast Volunteer Armies, stating: "The Northeast has been lost for eight months, and 30 million people are living under the trampling of Japanese imperialism every day. The government has consistently pursued a policy of non-resistance. The people of the Northeast, unable to endure any longer, realized that self-help was the only way to survive, and organized volunteer armies to fight against Japanese imperialism. However, the government ordered the prohibition of the organization of volunteer armies and obstructed the spiritual and material assistance of the people throughout the country to the Northeast Volunteer Armies. For several months, the Northeast Volunteer Armies have been fighting in difficult and arduous wars, suffering the slaughter of the violent Japanese and the destruction of Chinese traitors. They have been able to persevere and fight on, seeking liberation for the Chinese nation. This is due to the bravery of the soldiers and the support of the people throughout the country. Now, the violent Japanese are coveting the pass, and Tianjin and Beijing are in danger. The Shanghai Truce Agreement has been signed, and the government is willing to sell out the victory bought with the blood and flesh of the anti-Japanese soldiers of the 19th Route Army, and to sell out Shanghai, which controls the military and commercial lifeline of the whole country. The people of Shanghai will follow the people of the Northeast as slaves to a foreign country. Our association is organized by the Northeast people living in Shanghai. We have personally suffered the pain of losing our country and have no home to return to. The land where we reside has been sold by the government. Under the government's so-called long-term resistance, the Truce Agreement is a prelude to the future loss of the Northeast, and the people of the Northeast are a model for all the people of Shanghai and China. Our association deeply knows that the Japanese imperialists cannot be driven out of the country unless the people automatically arm themselves. Therefore, entrusted by 30 million people in the Northeast and the Northeast Volunteer Armies, we are conveying the oppression and hardship of the anti-Japanese war to the patriotic compatriots in Shanghai, requesting assistance and guidance from all sectors. We have decided to convene a tea party at our association's office at 25 Jiani Lane, Tongfu Road, at 2:00 PM on May 19. We hope that all sectors will attend enthusiastically and carry out practical assistance measures, so that the Northeast Volunteer Armies will have sufficient strength to drive out the violent Japanese and protect the Northeast, which is to protect the whole country. Our association has high hopes."

Important Domestic Telegrams

Ma Zhanshan's Troops Besiege Songpu Town

Intense Fighting Between the Two Armies, Cannon Fire Audible in Harbin

Four Bridges East of Yimianpo Were Destroyed by Fire

Foreign Dispatch Claims Hirose Division Entered Yilan City

(Harbin) In order to impede enemy troop movements, anti-Manchu forces yesterday morning doused four bridges fifteen miles east of Yimianpo with kerosene and then set them ablaze. They also attacked a repair train, but were repelled by machine gun fire from the train's guard. Several miles of railway tracks east of Hengdaohezi were also dismantled, so the recently restored transportation between Suifenhe and Hengdaohezi has now been disrupted again. The two armies fought fiercely today, vying for control of Songpu, near Harbin. Cannon fire was audible here. The anti-Manchu army advanced and heavily besieged the town, but has not yet breached it. The attackers used artillery, and their shells were quite accurate. Tonight, fires have broken out in various parts of the town, reminiscent of the devastating events in Zhabei in February. The attacking forces repeatedly retreated and advanced. It is reported that Ma Zhanshan's cavalry led the advance, but they have not yet succeeded. Three Japanese trains, escorted by armored vehicles, went to Hailin yesterday. It is reported that the Japanese army has occupied Erhe and Mudanjiang. Japanese troops stationed in Harbin were busy today piling up sandbag barricades in the new town, apparently in preparation for emergencies. (Reuters Dispatch, 17th)

Li Du's Army Moves Towards Fujin

(Tokyo) Pressed by the Japanese forces advancing along the Songhua River, Li Du's army decided to abandon Yilan and retreat towards Fujin, near the border between Eastern Province and Siberia. When withdrawing yesterday morning, they killed thirty-five Japanese residents. After the Nakamura Brigade entered the city, they discovered the bodies of the slain Japanese residents. The Japanese military authorities consider the occupation of this city to be an important victory. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

(Tokyo) According to newspaper reports, thirty-five Japanese residents of Yilan were killed by the anti-“Manchukuo” army commanded by Li Du. The anti-Manchu forces also set fire to the city before retreating towards Fujin. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

Hirose's Troops Enter Yilan City

(Harbin) The main force of the Hirose unit, led by two warships, sailed up the Songhua River and occupied Yilan yesterday. (Japanese League Dispatch, 18th)

(Harbin) The Hirose Division of the Japanese army occupied Yilan on the lower reaches of the Songhua River at 8:00 AM this morning. The division headquarters has moved into the city. (Dentsu Dispatch, 18th)

Two Military Authorities in Yuguan Plan Jointly to Resolve Misunderstandings

Matsushita Visits He Zhuguo

(Beiping) Yuguan Dispatch: Matsushita, commander of the garrison in Shanhaiguan, visited He Zhuguo this afternoon for two hours to discuss (1) ways to resolve past misunderstandings; (2) hoping newspapers will not exaggerate the Yuyu situation; (3) if pseudo-police and our police clash within the Great Wall, both sides will disarm and then negotiate; (4) the area outside the Great Wall is the responsibility of the Kwantung Army, and the garrison in Shanhaiguan is not responsible for any incidents that occur there; (5) the Chinese and Japanese sides will jointly maintain the security of Yuguan. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

(Beiping) Five members of the local militia, captured by the Japanese at Leshanpu, were released on the evening of the 17th after He Zhuguo’s intervention. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Conditions East of Yuyu Show No Signs of Easing

Shanhaiguan: The situation east of Yuyu shows no signs of easing. For several days, every passenger train on the pseudo-Fengshan Railway has been accompanied by two military freight cars. Troops have been increasing from Jinzhou to Suizhong. Armored vehicles have been running from Suizhong to Wanjiatun Station at night and leaving the next morning. Residents in all areas of former Wanjiatun cannot stay unless they have newly issued armbands. Yuguan was peaceful yesterday and today. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Japanese Side Restores Jinzhou Telegraph Bureau

Shanhaiguan: The Jinzhou Telegraph Bureau has been closed since the fall of Jinzhou. The Japanese military has ordered the rebels to send personnel to restore it. Now it is directly reporting to bureaus outside the Pass. However, the Suizhong Telegraph Bureau has been unable to directly report to bureaus inside the Pass since the 16th. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Japanese Army Builds Defense Works

(Beiping) A foreigner’s dispatch from Shanhaiguan: The Suzuki Brigade of the Japanese army has dispatched engineers to build defense works in the former garrison. Sandbags are piled up everywhere south of the Yuguan railway. Two Japanese destroyers arrived at Qinhuangdao on the 17th. Our troops are extremely calm. A certain military officer instructed his subordinates to remain calm and be patient in the face of provocations. If they are attacked, they should resist with all their might and be prepared to sacrifice themselves. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Japanese Troops Stationed in Beiping and Yuyu Will Be Replaced

(Tokyo) Vice Chief of Staff Masaki entered the palace at 11:30 this morning to report on the matter of rotating troops stationed in China and received the Emperor's approval. The troops being transferred back are three companies of infantry from the 9th Division in Kanazawa and two companies of infantry from the 5th Division in Hiroshima. The troops being sent to replace them are three companies of infantry from the 14th Division in Osaka and two companies of infantry from the 3rd Division in Nagoya. They will begin departing between the end of this month and the beginning of next month and will be stationed in Beiping, Shanhaiguan, Qinhuangdao, and other places. (Dentsu Dispatch, 18th)

Issue of Restoring Sino-Russian Relations

Opinion of a Certain Important Diplomatic Figure

(Nanjing) A certain important diplomatic figure said that relations between China and the Soviet Union have been intermittent for several years. The Sino-Soviet conference has stalled, not only due to the Manchurian Incident, but also because the contents of the three matters of the Eastern Railway, restoration of communications, and commerce are complex and cannot be resolved in the short term. The Central Government is carefully studying the major policy toward Russia. Although there has been some indirect contact recently, it has not yet materialized. The outside world believes that restoring relations with Russia is tantamount to accommodating communism, but this is not the case. Many countries that have diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union do not accommodate communism, and this is one example. However, there is a prerequisite for restoring relations with Russia: mutual recognition that it does not hinder the political security and social organization of each country. The basis of diplomatic relations should be built on mutual commerce and the restoration of normal diplomatic relations, such as embassies and consulates, so that the consulates in the border provinces of Eastern Province and the coastal provinces of the Soviet Union, which have been de facto closed since 1930, are willing to be restored. Therefore, restoring diplomatic relations with Russia today is not difficult in exchanging a document, but the difficulty lies in whether the prerequisite is acceptable to the other party. The Mo representative sent a telegram from Brussels, saying that he is planning a trip to Paris. If the Central Government decides on a major policy toward Russia, Mo can return to Russia and deal with the Soviet authorities. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Refutation of Russian Newspaper Editorial

(Nanjing) A spokesperson for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today refuted an editorial published in the Moscow Izvestia newspaper on May 13 regarding Sino-Russian relations, stating that although Mr. Mo Hui has temporarily left Moscow, the Chinese delegation is still stationed in that city. The statement in the newspaper that the Chinese delegation has ceased to exist by order of the National Government is unfounded. The spokesperson also mentioned the issue of restoring Sino-Russian relations, saying that the tone of the Russian newspaper's remarks made it difficult to promote friendly relations between the two countries. (Reuters Dispatch, 18th)

Chen Yinghshi Martyrdom

16th Anniversary Commemoration

Central Party Headquarters

(Beiping) Luoyang Dispatch: On the morning of the 18th, the Central Party Headquarters held a commemoration for Chen Yinghshi. More than 600 people attended. Chairman Dai, Yao Yuping, Niu Yongjian, and Dai Chuanxian successively reported on Chen Yinghshi's deeds and the circumstances they witnessed during the uprising and his martyrdom. The audience was moved. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Central Government Office in Nanjing

(Nanjing) The Central Government Office in Nanjing held the 16th anniversary commemoration of Mr. Chen Yinghshi's martyrdom on the morning of the 18th. More than 500 people attended, including Central Committee members Zhang Ji, Wang Zhaoming, Jiang Zhongzheng, Ju Zheng, Ye Chucang, Chen Guofu, Shao Yuanchong, Qin Zhen, and Chen Shuren, as well as staff and guests. Ju Zheng presided and Shao Yuanchong gave a report, briefly saying that recalling the tragic death of Mr. Yinghshi in Shanghai in 1916 made them feel very sad and inspired. After the failure of the Second Revolution in 1913, many comrades lost their courage. Only Mr. Yinghshi recognized the cause of the failure and strongly helped President Sun Yat-sen reorganize the Chinese Revolutionary Party, which was established in 1914. After returning to China from Japan, Mr. Yinghshi immediately engaged in preparing for activities in the Northeast and then went to Shanghai to preside over military affairs along the Yangtze River coast, vowing never to flee overseas again. At that time, Shanghai was under the military pressure of Yuan Shikai, and the environment was very bad. However, Mr. Yinghshi had made the greatest determination and courage and had no intention of retreating or shrinking back. At that time, some comrades in the headquarters could not understand Mr. Yinghshi's difficulties, and some comrades in Shanghai also organized separate activities, which greatly affected the revolutionary movement led by Mr. Yinghshi. Mr. Yinghshi had already made the determination to die for the country and fight forward. After the failure of the Zhaohuo warship uprising in December 1915, the revolution became even more difficult. Chen was willing to sacrifice his own life to promote the success of the revolution. On this day in 1916, Chen was killed in Shanghai by Li Haiqiu, a member of the rebel party, who was instructed by Yuan Shikai, Feng Guozhang, Zhang Zongchang, and others, and orchestrated seven or eight murderers to break into his residence. Mr. Chen died for the country in a very short time. Mr. Chen's determination to die for the country is the foundation of the spirit of all revolutionary comrades and the key to the success of the revolutionary party. Mr. Chen believed in the principles of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and practiced them diligently, giving them a model instruction. They should have revolutionary confidence and courage to make the foundation of all activities. The revival of the Chinese nation must be based on the President's revolutionary strategy and principles in order to succeed. The President advocated the revolutionary army movement, not hoping to succeed in his own lifetime, but only to point out to the people of the country a broad road to save the country and the people. Under the guidance of the President's spirit, revolutionary comrades should have confidence and courage, be determined to succeed or die, follow in the footsteps of the martyrs, and move forward bravely. Then they will not fear how strong the reactionary forces are or how dangerous the country is. They can remove all obstacles and achieve great success. They commemorate Mr. Chen and, of course, are sad, but they should encourage each other in this spirit of sadness, cultivate and train themselves, and can complete the success of the future revolution. (Central Telegraph, 18th)

Special Party Headquarters of the Military Academy

(Nanjing) The Special Party Headquarters of the Central Military Academy held a commemoration for Chen Yinghshi on the morning of the 18th. More than 200 people attended. Li Zhengeng presided, and Mi Ouchi reported on Chen Yisheng's deeds and the points to be emulated. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 18th)

Beiping Municipal Party Headquarters

(Nanjing) The Municipal Party Headquarters held a memorial for Chen Yinghshi's martyrdom on the 18th. Lou Tongsun gave a speech, saying that the party's confidence and the party members' loyalty and integrity must be restored. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

(Beiping) The Municipal Party Headquarters held a commemoration for Chen Qimei's martyrdom this morning. (Special Dispatch, 18th)

Foreign Important Telegrams

British Government Decides

To Complete Singapore Naval Base

Prime Minister of New Zealand Declares

Reuters, Wellington, 18th. New Zealand Prime Minister Forbes declared here today that the Singapore naval base must be built. A firm decision has now been made, and the New Zealand government does not wish to reduce its share of the expenses. He also stated that the Parliamentary Expenditure Committee proposed that New Zealand's naval defenses be handed over to the British government, but the New Zealand government decided not to accept this proposal.

Belgian Cabinet Resigns

National News Agency, Brussels, 17th. The Belgian cabinet resigned today due to the long-standing dispute over the use of the Flemish language. The Belgian people consist of two groups: the Flemish and the Walloons (descendants of the Salian Franks residing in northern Flanders). The Flemish speak Flemish, and their numbers are slightly greater than the Walloons. Belgium has traditionally used French as the official language, but after the Flemish fought for it, both French and Flemish were used as official languages.

National News Agency, Brussels, 17th. Although the language issue is the reason for the resignation of the Belgian cabinet, it is now believed that the recent discovery by Parliament that Belgian Prime Minister Renkin was involved in a corruption case concerning the construction of the Antwerp Canal is not unrelated to the cabinet's resignation.

French Army Chief

Falls into the Sea During Flight and is Rescued

National News Agency, Paris, 18th. French Army Chief General Pittri was flying to Corsica last night when his engine malfunctioned and he landed in the sea. Unfortunately, the rescue plane also crashed while landing, and the pilot was injured. Both planes drifted in the sea, but luckily a cruiser spotted them and rescued the Army Chief. Another ship towed both planes back to Toulon.

After Conflicts Between Hindus and Muslims

A desolate scene in Bombay

Reuters, Bombay, 18th. After dusk last night, the entire city was silent. Theaters and restaurants were closed, and there were no pedestrians on the streets. Every few steps, British soldiers stood in the shadows. The usually bustling area now presents a desolate scene. What makes people still remember the terror of the past three days of unrest are the fires that can be seen everywhere on the streets, still smoldering, and the broken storefronts and the scattered items on the road. Boxes and other items are piled up everywhere on the main streets, as if commemorating a dishonorable outburst.

Reuters, Bombay, 17th. Conflicts between Hindus and Muslims here since last Saturday and Sunday have resulted in 88 deaths and 850 injuries. However, after the deployment of British troops, the situation has calmed down somewhat. Although Muslims still occasionally fight with Hindus while celebrating the New Year, the authorities have gradually been able to maintain order. The police and soldiers have shown no bias towards either religious group. An order has been issued prohibiting nighttime travel and gatherings of more than five people. During a parade by Muslims in Calcutta today, they were pelted with stones by Hindus, causing a conflict. Many police officers were also hit by objects while trying to suppress the riot, and more than a dozen civilians were injured. However, order was soon restored.

Lindbergh is Deceived after Loss of Son

Reuters, Hopewell, 17th. Amidst the grief of losing his son, the Lindbergh couple was shocked to learn that the person they had entrusted to negotiate with the kidnappers was actually a con artist. This person is Curtis, the "Norfolk Millionaire Shipowner" reported in the newspapers. The Lindbergh couple regarded Curtis as a trustworthy person and trusted him completely, but unexpectedly he took the opportunity to defraud them, causing them to be misled. According to the New Jersey Sheriff, after being interrogated for several hours, Curtis confessed that he had fabricated the story of contacting the kidnappers because a newspaper and a film company offered him a large sum of money for exclusive news about the kidnapping case. Curtis further stated that he had completely written down the beginning and end of his scam on a typewriter at 4:00 this morning and sent it to the sheriff. He claimed that his shipbuilding business had gone bankrupt last year, and he had been experiencing financial difficulties recently. He admitted that he had been blinded by greed and had done something inhumane, which was not his original intention. The New Jersey Sheriff stated that the police department's investigation was disrupted by Curtis's scam, and the detectives had to make many unnecessary trips, and Colonel Lindbergh was unable to stay home and handle everything during the most important period.

Gogulov

Mental Derangement Before the Assassination

National News Agency, Paris, 17th. Gogulov, the assassin of French President Doumer, was subjected to a rigorous interrogation again today. According to the results, the French authorities now believe that the case was the result of an individual's actions and was not related to any political organization or movement. Gogulov no longer exhibits manic behavior and freely answers all questions. It is said that since he arrived in Paris three days before the assassination, he had been in a daze all day, his mind filled with the idea of assassinating the president and killing himself with the last bullet. Sometimes he was slightly more lucid and decided to abandon this sinister plan, praying at Notre Dame Cathedral. At other times, he drank heavily, hoping to forget everything. Even before the assassination, he drank several bottles of brandy in several cafes, hoping that he could forget his assassination plan after getting drunk. However, he was unable to achieve his wish and shot the president in a drunken stupor. However, he had two guns in his pocket at the time and had completely forgotten which gun he used to carry out the assassination. As for his motive for the assassination, it was because France seemed unwilling to attack Soviet Russia, which made him extremely angry and mad. He believed that the French president represented the French government, so he wanted to die with him.

Important News

Osaka Mainichi Shimbun on

The Imminence of a US-Japan War

This article first discusses the difficulties of the United States in fighting in the Pacific. First, the morale of the navy is weak. Second, the strength of the fleet is insufficient. Third, the fleet is difficult to mobilize and coordinate, giving the impression that it is vulnerable to attack. Next, it discusses the US naval exercises as a challenge to Japan. The US changing its planned course of action and stationing its fleet indefinitely in the Pacific is something the Japanese cannot tolerate. The danger in US-Japan relations is clear from this article.

The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun published an article by Tadataka Ikezeki on the 12th of this month, entitled "The Fateful US-Japan War." The article is very long. Here is the translation:

According to a Washington dispatch on April 14, the United States is holding large-scale naval exercises in the Pacific, with all US fleets participating. At the same time, the US State Department plans to have the reconnaissance fleet dispatched from the Atlantic to guard the Pacific indefinitely after the end of the exercises. It has consulted the naval authorities on this idea. Although the naval authorities have not yet formally ordered its implementation, they are already preparing for it. This US naval exercise is commanded by General Schofield, and it will be based on the idea of holding a joint army and navy defense exercise centered on the US Pacific coast and the Hawaiian Islands on February 6. Therefore, its scale is larger than the naval exercises held in 1925. According to the New York Times, the exercise will continue for 97 days from February 6 to May 13, divided into three phases. The first phase is from February 6 to February 11. The Pacific Coast Battle Fleet and the army forces stationed in Hawaii will participate in a joint army and navy defense exercise centered on Hawaii. The second phase is from March 8 to March 23. The Battle Fleet departing from Hawaii will advance toward the US West Coast to obtain a base. After March 8, the reconnaissance fleet scheduled to arrive in the waters between San Francisco and Vancouver will practice resisting real combat. The third phase is from March 23 to May 13. After the end of the second phase, the Battle Fleet and the Reconnaissance Fleet will be combined to conduct fleet concentration exercises and various combat skills training in the waters off San Francisco and Vancouver. According to the planned schedule, the Reconnaissance Fleet of the Atlantic forces of the US Combined Fleet, commanded by Vice Admiral Vitter, will also set sail from its various bases in the Atlantic, call at Guantanamo, the US Navy's winter base in Cuba, and conduct shooting exercises. In early March, the air squadron and destroyer squadron, which took separate actions from the main force, will gather at the port of Vancouver, a base on the Pacific coast.

However, according to the telegram issued on April 14, the planned schedule seems to have been changed, and the three phases of the exercise have ended. What kind of effect the sudden shortening of the implementation period of the large-scale exercise has is not something that can be guessed. It is rumored that many sailors believed that war with Japan would break out during the large-scale exercise, and they were quite worried. As a result, as many as 1,500 crew members deserted from the US fleet. In addition, the battle fleet moored in Hawaii had an inappropriate incident involving soldiers landing on the island, which led to the issue of prohibiting landings. From this point of view, the weakening of the morale of the US fleet is difficult to deny. What I (Ikezaki) want to point out urgently is that the US State Department suddenly declared that after the large-scale exercise, the reconnaissance fleet dispatched from the Atlantic will be deployed indefinitely in the Pacific, which is unprecedented. We speculate that they must believe that an accident will occur in the Pacific, or that an accident will brew in the Pacific. Therefore, this action is a strategy to threaten the opposing enemy. The actions expressed by the US government have gone beyond the norm, and holding naval exercises is even more of an extraordinary action. (To be continued)

Japanese Government

Changes Policy Toward Russia

Striving to Eliminate Misunderstandings

First Achieve Economic Compromise

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reports that after Foreign Minister Yoshizawa obtained a detailed report from former Ambassador to Russia Tatsukichi Tanaka after his return from an inspection of Manchuria, he urgently wanted to change his policy toward Russia in view of the deterioration of the situation in the Far East in order to avoid unrest in Northern Manchuria. At present, in order to establish a policy toward Russia, there are two opinions among influential people within the government on how to deal with it: (1) The issue of a non-aggression treaty with Russia: Before this kind of political issue is resolved, it is advocated that an economic policy toward Russia be established first, but a gradual approach is adopted for economic issues with Russia, and a wait-and-see attitude is still taken; (2) General policy toward Russia: The government strives to eliminate the causes of misunderstandings between the two countries and improve the national relations between the two countries. (Note: At present, Japan's enemies are Russia and the United States. Since Russia concentrated a large army on the border of Northern Manchuria, the situation between Japan and Russia has suddenly become dangerous, but the anti-American sentiment in Japan is more severe than the anti-Russian sentiment. If Japan wants to start a war with the United States, it has to ease relations with Russia. This change in policy toward Russia is a preparation for actively opposing the United States.)

Japanese

Coveting the Resources of Mongolia and Manchuria

Also Sends People to Mongolia to Explore Resources 　　Decides to Exploit Manchurian Aluminum Ore 　　Dalian Communication: The Japanese are extremely meticulous in their reconnaissance of Mongolia and Manchuria. Last year there was Nakamura, and this year there is Matsui, who entered Mongolia and Manchuria to explore. Now there are also Kirita and Ikemoto, who are going to Mongolia to search for all kinds of materials. The two are preparing to depart, starting last November. This February, they will actually set off from Nagoya, Japan, and go to Inner Mongolia on foot. They arrived in Hamgyongnam-do, Korea on April 3, and departed from Hoeryong, Korea on the morning of the 5th, passing through Yanji to enter Dunhua, and crossing the large forest of the Furul Ridge. They are expected to cross Qiqihar and the Hinggan Mountains in October of this year, and arrive in Mongolia in December. They plan to return to Liaoning in July next year. The journey is a total of 4,134 kilos, and the work schedule is estimated to be 430 days. I hope that our compatriots will pay close attention to it.

Aluminum is an important raw material for manufacturing aircraft. At present, military and civilian aircraft in various countries around the world mostly use aluminum to manufacture their bodies and wings. This mineral is extremely precious in the world. Except for the United States and France, other countries have not seen much of it. Northeast China is rich in this mineral, and the Japanese have been coveting it for many years. Now, in preparation for actual mining, the Japanese government has sent Dr. Takaoka, director of the Osaka Municipal Industrial Research Institute, to Northeast China to investigate and conduct field tests. It is reported that the mining areas have been discovered, including Fuzhou, Daweijiadun, Benxihu, Yantai, and Tian Yang Fu Man. The total reserves in these five locations are 150 million tons, with a mineral composition of approximately 40%, and a large amount of potassium sulfate can be extracted. All of the aluminum materials currently used in Japan are imported from France, with an annual demand of 12,000 tons, costing more than 10 million yuan. The reason why the Japanese are eager to exploit the aluminum ore in Northeast China is that, on the one hand, they can stop the outflow of economic resources, and on the other hand, they can gain a great military advantage. If all five of these mining areas are exploited, they can supply the entire world for 200 years. (May 14)

Ma Zhanshan Telegraphed the Investigation Team Again

Exposing Japanese Conspiracy

Announcing a Forged Agreement Forced Upon Under Duress by the Japanese

Preventing Redization Is No Concern of the Japanese

Beiping Correspondence: After Ma Zhanshan arrived in Heihe last month, he sent a telegram to the national investigation team exposing the Japanese plot in the Northeast. It is now learned that Mr. Ma sent another telegram to the team on April 17, detailing everything and attaching the "Hu-Hai Railway Heihe Provincial Official Bank Resumption Loan Contract" and the "Sino-Japanese Joint Aviation Transport Contract," which were forced upon by the Japanese. The official announcement of these extremely important documents was made yesterday. The full text is recorded below:

Full text of Ma Zhanshan's telegram to Director Zhang Suijing, please forward to Chairman Lytton and all members of the League of Nations Investigation Team: My previous telegram was brief and the meaning unclear. Now, I will further explain to your team. Since the Japanese invasion of the Northeast, they know that their violent aggression is unacceptable to the civilized international community of the 20th century. They use sophistry to deceive the world, repeatedly claiming that they are dispatching troops to protect expatriates or that China is unable to curb the redization of Soviet Russia and must take action to prevent it in order to contain the chaos in the world. However, in reality, local officials in various places have spared no effort to protect expatriates in China. Even though the public deeply resent the Japanese for their various acts of brutality and unreasonableness, and there are occasional boycotts, the government has always curbed these actions to prevent them from exceeding the limit. As a result, no Japanese expatriates have been killed. Even after the September 18th Incident in Liaoning last year, our country still protected non-combatant Japanese as usual. This shows that China has always valued justice and humanity, does not harbor revenge, and can endure what others cannot. The League of Nations is far away in Geneva and may not be aware of these details. However, the consuls of the British and American embassies and the resident groups in Harbin have conducted actual investigations. The envoys have reported fairly on their visits to places as far west as Manzhouli. On the other hand, the Japanese have massacred our innocent civilians, such as in the Jinan Massacre and the Wanbaoshan Korean Incident, killing thousands at a time. The massacres in Liaoning last year, and the killings of civilians in Shanghai Jiangwan, Zhabei, etc., this year, are all inhumane acts that have been seen and heard by the international community. As for redization, the Chinese government has always adopted a policy of active prevention. The Northeast borders Soviet Russia, especially Heilongjiang Province, where the border is contiguous. The prevention is tight, and the inspection of red literature and printed matter is strict to prevent them from flowing in. Commerce is also being considered, and a blockade policy is still in effect. I, Zhanshan, have been governing the army along the border for many years and have strictly prohibited redization. The people along the border also regard redization as terrible and avoid it like snakes and scorpions. For example, during the Nenjiang Bridge battle, the Japanese side claimed that our army had the assistance of Soviet Russia. In fact, not only were there no Soviet Russian officers participating in the entire army, but there were also no White Russians joining. The Soviet Russian side also felt that they were too busy to take care of themselves and tried their best to avoid any suspicion of joining hands with us. It can be seen that the Japanese propaganda is purely to deceive the world. Our country has a real grasp of preventing redization and does not need the Japanese to overstep their bounds and plan for us. This time, I, Zhanshan, saw through the Japanese conspiracy and, in order to save the country, led troops to Heihe to carry out righteous resistance. The Japanese then spread propaganda that it was related to a certain country, disregarding our nation's inability to resist. If there is resistance, it is said that there must be external forces. As a great power, they have resorted to such rogue propaganda to deceive the world and disrupt peace. They do not know that in recent years, the world view and national thought of the Chinese people are completely different from the time when the Boxers disturbed the country thirty years ago. Anyone from other countries who is slightly familiar with the Chinese situation will be able to understand the Japanese embellishments and sophistry, which are nothing more than tools for aggression and will be self-defeating. The League of Nations is the only arbitration mechanism for maintaining world peace. The investigation team bears the important mission of coming to China to investigate, nothing more than to understand the details and truth. It is hoped that the most accurate observations will be made and the most impartial report will be issued, so that ambitious countries will not be able to achieve their cunning plans. This will not only solve the Sino-Japanese problem, but also ensure lasting world peace. The various contracts and agreements that the Japanese forced upon us but have not been signed are listed separately on the left for your inspection.

Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, Ma Zhanshan.

Resumption Fund Contract Regarding the loan contract for the resumption fund of the Official Bank of Heilongjiang Province, the Heilongjiang Provincial Government and the South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd. hereby enter into a contract regarding the loan for the resumption fund of the Official Bank of Heilongjiang Province: (Article 1) The company will lend the provincial government 3 million Japanese yen as the resumption fund for the Official Bank. (Article 2) The term of the loan is 50 years. (Article 3) The loan interest rate is set at 7.5% per annum, that is, 7 yen and 50 sen per 100 yen per year. From the date of signing this contract, it will be paid every six months from the income of the Hu-Hai Railway. No interest will be paid on interest that cannot be paid on time, but the delayed interest will be paid first from the remaining funds for the payment of the annual interest for that year. (Article 4) The loan principal will be repaid annually from the income of the Hu-Hai Railway according to a separately determined repayment schedule, but it may not be fully repaid before the expiration date. (Article 5) All movable and immovable property and all income of the Hu-Hai Railway now and in the future shall be the guarantee for the principal and interest of this loan, and shall not be the guarantee for debts other than this contract. (Article 6) The provincial government entrusts the company with the operation of the Hu-Hai Railway. (Article 7) This contract shall take effect upon signing. (Article 8) This contract shall be written in duplicate in Chinese and Japanese, and the provincial government and the company shall each keep one copy as proof. In case of any doubt in the interpretation of this contract, the Japanese version shall prevail. Month and day of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Month and day of the 7th year of Showa, Ma Zhanshan, Governor of Heilongjiang Province, Yasuya Uchida, President of South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd.

Hu-Hai Railway Contract Heilongjiang Province and South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd., based on the provisions of the Heilongjiang Provincial Official Bank Resumption Fund Loan Contract, conclude the Hu-Hai Railway Operation Contract as follows: (Article 1) The Provincial Government entrusts the Company with all matters related to the operation of the Hu-Hai Railway. (Article 2) The Provincial Government shall appoint a Director to be responsible for the supervision of this railway. (Article 3) The Company shall appoint a representative to be responsible for all matters related to the operation of this railway. (Article 4) The salary of the Director and the Company Representative shall be agreed upon by the Provincial Government and the Company. (Article 5) The salary of the Director's staff, as well as their appointment, dismissal, and promotion, shall be determined by the Director, but the amount of funds required shall be agreed upon by the Director and the Company Representative. (Article 6) If the total income of this railway is not enough to cover the operating expenses of the year, the Company shall supplement it free of charge, but special expenses due to incidents and other force majeure shall be agreed upon at that time. (Article 7) 5% (seems to be missing words or wrong here) of the profit of this railway will be used as operating expenses, in addition to the new equipment and improvements other than the existing equipment. 30% will be allocated to the Provincial Government and 20% to the Company. The various profits refer to the interest in the total income up to the expenses for the interest of that year, up to the remaining funds for the delayed interest of that year, and the principal payable for that year. When the amount received by the Provincial Government stipulated in the first item is less than 6/1000 of the total amount of the debt of the Heilongjiang Official Bank Resumption Fund Loan Contract, the Company shall fill the difference to the Provincial Government up to 6/1000. (Article 8) This railway must be connected to the Qike Railway, and in the future, Harbin will be the starting point or the end point. Only the newly built railway will be operated together with these two railways. (Article 9) When constructing the connecting line and its branch line or extension line of this railway, the company shall select and dispatch a chief engineer to be responsible. The funds required for its construction office shall be borrowed by the company. (Article 10) When the operating expenses stipulated on the right are insufficient, they can be borrowed by the company. The loans in the first two items shall be treated as additional... The interest shall be handled in the same way as the loan interest in the Heilongjiang Provincial Official Bank Resumption Fund Loan Contract. (Article 11) Regarding the existing claims and debts of the Hu-Hai Railway at the time of the establishment of this contract, another agreement will be made. (Article 12) This contract shall take effect when the Heilongjiang Provincial Official Bank Resumption Fund Loan Contract is established. (Article 13) This contract shall be written in duplicate in Chinese and Japanese, and the provincial government and the company shall each keep one copy as proof. In case of any doubt in the interpretation of this contract, the Japanese version shall prevail. Month and day of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Month and day of the 7th year of Showa, Ma Zhanshan, Governor of Heilongjiang Province, Yasuya Uchida, President of South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd.

Aviation Transportation Contract (Copy) Sino-Japanese Joint Aviation Transportation Business Contract. Ma Zhanshan is Party A and Lin Yixiu is Party B. Both Parties, regarding the transportation of passengers and goods by aircraft, conclude the following business contract: (1) This aviation transportation business shall be handled by the joint investment of Chinese and Japanese businessmen. (2) The Chinese side shall provide all necessary equipment and aircraft for this aviation business. (3) The management method of this aviation business shall be decided by the joint agreement of Parties A and B. As for the implementation of the business, it shall be undertaken by Party B. (4) The profits and losses arising from this aviation business shall be shared equally by Parties A and B. (5) The term of validity of this contract shall be calculated from March 1st of Datong 1st year, and shall be set for five years first. Upon expiration, it may be continued after consultation between Parties A and B. (6) This contract shall be recorded in Chinese and Japanese, and each party shall keep a copy. This contract shall be put into trial flight after both parties sign and seal it. Established on March 1st of Datong 1st year, Ma Zhanshan, Lin Yixiu. (Note) Explanation of Aviation Transportation Business Contract: (1) The meaning of the provision in Article 2 of the Sino-Japanese Joint Aviation Transportation Business Contract that all necessary equipment and aircraft must be supplied refers to Party A supplying the airport. (2) Although it is said that the profits and losses arising from the business shall be shared equally by both parties, Party B shall bear all damages and shall not allow Party A to bear them. (3) The route of the air route starts from Harbin, passes through Qiqihar, to Manzhouli line, so airports will be built in Harbin and Manzhouli. Then, opportunities will be sought to build the Qiqihar via Nennjiang to (missing five words here) Heihe line, and the Harbin via Hailun to Heihe line. Currently, airports will be built in Nenjiang Heihe and Hailun first. The explanation on the right is exchanged on March 1st of Datong 1st year, Ma Zhanshan, Lin Yixiu.

Imprisonment for Counterfeiting Tickets The Minsheng Printing House on Jingde Road, Suzhou City

The Minsheng Printing House on Jingde Road, Suzhou City, counterfeited public bond tickets last year. Later, the Ministry of Finance found out and sent personnel to secretly investigate and verify the facts. They telegraphed the Wu County Public Security Bureau to arrest Cha Nianchun, the director of the printing house, and seized a large number of printed public bond tickets. The Public Security Bureau immediately sent Cha to the Wu County Local Court for investigation and prosecution. Yesterday, the court pronounced its verdict, sentencing Cha Nianchun to three years of fixed-term imprisonment and a fine of 300 yuan.

Important News

The Government Returned Xiaozhuang Normal School

Preparing for a Children's Science Summer School

The Nanjing Xiaozhuang Normal School, run by Tao Xingzhi, advocated rural experimental education and achieved remarkable results. For a time, schools across the country took it as a model, and many followed suit. In recent years, Mr. Tao has felt even more that to save the country and the people, it is necessary to promote scientific knowledge and skills, so that our nation has scientific knowledge and skills in order to adapt to modern life and survive in the modern world. The fundamental way to promote the scientific intelligence of the nation is to train children in science. Therefore, Mr. Tao has gathered many comrades in the past year to compile 100 kinds of children's science series, which will be published by the Children's Art Library before this summer. At this time, the government has clearly ordered the return of Xiaozhuang Normal School. Elementary schools and kindergartens within 40 miles around Xiaozhuang have opened one after another, and it has been decided to establish a large-scale children's science summer school in Xiaozhuang from July 15 to August 15, specializing in the study of children's natural science with a quota of 1,000 people. Recruit university graduates, science teachers from various normal schools, and teachers from various elementary schools. The city and county supervisors will study separately and hope that summer schools for children's science research will appear in the township next summer. After one year, the proposition of children's natural science can be promoted throughout the country. The summer school research courses are divided into ten types: (1) Children's Biology, (2) Children's Chemistry, (3) Children's Earth, (4) Children's Physics, (5) Children's Astronomy, (6) Children's Geometry, (7) Children's Agronomy, (8) Children's Crafts, (9) Children's Physiology and Hygiene, (10) Children's Science Guidance.

The Ministry of Education Advocated Changing to Building Military Aircraft

The Zhejiang Education Department submitted the articles of association of the Hangzhou Branch of the China Children's Savings to Build Ships to Save the Country Association and a book on children's warships, requesting the Ministry of Education to order all provinces and cities to follow suit. It is also hoped that the method of keeping the savings will be properly formulated.

Shanghai's Educational Undertakings After January 28th (7) Still

Two Institutions Set Up Cram Schools… Boy Scouts are Commendable for Their Loyalty and Bravery

7. Remedial Classes During the War

Since the enemy troops pressed into Shanghai, all education, whether in the war zone or non-war zone, whether in universities or elementary schools, was in a state of suspension. Especially university education. Therefore, the Business School of Central University added remedial night classes, the Shanghai YMCA prepared university cram schools, and the Chinese Vocational Education College attached university and middle school remedial courses to relieve those young men and women who were hungry for knowledge.

Now, let us introduce the content and methods of the university and middle school remedial courses attached to the Chinese Vocational Education Society, so as to understand the general situation of Shanghai's cram schools after January 28th. At the same time, we pray that the Chinese people will strive for success so as not to have another tragedy like this of temporarily embracing Buddha's feet. The purpose of the remedial courses attached to the Vocational Education Society is, needless to say, to relieve the general out-of-school youth, so that the youth have the opportunity to learn, so as to avoid wasting their studies and wasting time. The level is divided into two groups in the undergraduate course, one is for students in the first and second grades of the university, and one group is for students in the second and third grades of high school. Subjects: The middle school group sets up four subjects: Chinese, English, Mathematics, Physics and Chemistry. Scholars are also invited to give special lectures. The university group sets up four subjects: Chinese, English, Mathematics, Social Science (including Political Science, Economics, Education, and Sociology), and scholars are also invited to give special lectures. The class period is tentatively set for four months, from March 1st to June 30th. The teaching time is six days a week for each group, and four hours of classes a day. The university group is from 8:00 am to 12:00 pm, and the middle school group is from 1:00 pm to 5:00 pm. The quota is tentatively set at 100 middle school students and 50 university students, both male and female. If each group is less than 35 people, the class will not be opened. Tuition: University students pay 30 yuan, and middle school students pay 24 yuan. A fee for handouts will be charged at the discretion of those who use handouts. If the war ends and the schools open, it will be stopped immediately. The tuition fee will be refunded proportionally according to the date of instruction. Registration: Those who are interested in learning can report to the Chinese Vocational Education Society at the intersection of Hualong Road and Huanlong Road from February 23rd to February 29th, and pay a registration fee of 5 yuan, which will be deducted from the tuition fee. The school will start on March 1st. Certificates: At the end of June, students who pass the exam will receive a certificate of completion. They have seven members: Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, Chen Xuanshan, Shen Yougan, Pan Wenan, Jia Foru, and Wu Cuilun. Chen Xuanshan presides over the teaching affairs. They received a total of 154 male students and 35 female students. The university group did not open a class because the number of people was not enthusiastic. An extra junior high school class was added, which was a later change.

The YMCA's university cram school is located in the French Concession's Baixianqiao. Chen Liting is in charge of all affairs, and university professors such as Pan Guangdan and Xie Xunchu help him to succeed. Liu Zhanen, the president of Shanghai University, also took the time to help. Their nature is completely based on the lecture system, which is similar to the "University Free Lecture System" advocated by Liang Qichao in the past. There were more than 130 people who went to listen to the lectures by subject, and they were all good young people who admired that every inch of time is worth every inch of gold. The evening business school added by Shanghai University on Bowuyuan Road is intended to encourage aspiring young people to have remedial intentions, which can be compared with Soochow Law School before and after, and it opened urgently during the war.

11. Scouting

Unexpectedly, the shocking news that Jin...the rivers and mountains of the Northeast had been lost by soldiers who did not fight and lands that were not defended spread to Shanghai. The reporter proposed to set up a "Scout Battlefield Service Committee" at the council of the highest scouting authority. This committee was established, and it was discussed several times, and everything was prepared. Who knew that they did not go to the Northeast, and nearby Shanghai was as alarmed as the Northeast. On the day after the January 28th Incident, most of the Christians and victims took refuge in the Muer Church, a haven of peace. It was late at night and cold, and many victims could not sleep, and often hugged each other to keep warm. The Muer Church's scouts could not bear to see this tragic situation, and that night they rushed to Jinrong Elementary School to borrow blankets. The beneficiaries still remember this kind deed of giving charcoal in the snow.

Starting from borrowing blankets, the Boy Scouts expanded the scope of services and set off for the battlefield. On January 30th, the coaching team run by the council and the 270th scout regiment of Muer Church began to be active, and recruited more than 600 people who volunteered to join the army, and established the "Battlefield Service Team". Wang Gang was elected as the commander-in-chief, and Xi Xueqiao, Luo Lie, Wang Yiqiao, and girl scout Huang Shan were elected as deputies. Yu Julu, director of the organization department, Chen Tao, director of the general affairs department, Zhu Jiarang, director of the document department, He Jia, director of the propaganda department, Ni Jiaxi, captain of the rescue team, and Feng Zhenwei, captain of the labor team, were also appointed. They went to fight for survival for the motherland with great momentum and to seize the rivers and mountains.

Their rescue work rescued more than 700 compatriots in the front line of Zhabei, like fish out of water and prisoners awaiting execution. They set up 13 refugee shelters in the rear, and served in more than 20 other shelters and hospitals, specializing in the management of security affairs. The vehicles of the 19th Route Army came in and out and the management of comfort items also relied on them, and the order was well-organized.

When the war was raging, there was a shortage of personnel to deliver messages in the front. The scouts immediately selected 12 people who were good at driving skills to form a "Front Message Delivery Team" led by Ni Jiaxi to deliver important documents to the transportation office of the Zhenru Headquarters. They entered and exited the smoke-filled fire, without any fear or trepidation. The planes soared and circled overhead to track them down, and the roar of cannons and the arrows of bullets flew up and down, left and right, shocking them, but they never delayed official business. Commander-in-chief Jiang Guangnai and Commander Cai Tingkai saw their loyalty and bravery and their excellent achievements, and they all applauded and praised them, and asked the scouts to serve in the Nanchang Headquarters. Wang Gang added 25 people and asked Feng Zhenwei to lead them to do the work that people were unwilling to do and dared not do.

Central University Medical School Largely Destroyed

As our troops defended the second line of defense, the reception centers set up by the Boy Scouts gradually closed. The remaining scouts and 270 new members were trained by Wang Gang and Zhao Weizu, who taught battlefield skills. They became the third batch of front-line service personnel. Detouring to Kunshan, after being addressed by Tang Dehuang, the chief of the traffic department of the 19th Route Army headquarters, they joined the first and second batches of Boy Scouts in road construction, supervision, bridge building, reconnaissance, transportation, reception, and communication. The installation of telegraph poles and wires from Kunshan to Changshu was all done by them. It is said that they completed this work in a week. The digging of trenches around the city wall of Suzhou was done in cooperation with the Feng Da's Volunteer Army and the Skull Squad. Now, the Boy Scouts are solely responsible. Their communication and reconnaissance areas include Nanjing and the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou roads, where they left many footprints. Their permanent locations are Suzhou, Songjiang, Zhengyi, Kunshan, Wuxi, Nanxiang, and Zhenru. The "Boy Scout Military Affairs Office" is their command center and the general headquarters for issuing orders. The 50th Regiment Boy Scouts of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce should operate independently. They have also made many contributions, but unfortunately, several comrades died from stray bullets. The names of these comrades have not yet been discovered. We should silently mourn those who have passed away.

When the League of Nations investigation team arrived in Nanjing, Chairman Lord Lytton did nothing. The first thing he did was to summon the Boy Scouts at the Lixingshe for a lecture. Some important Chinese figures were inevitably surprised. It turned out that Lytton was the forefather of the Boy Scouts and a student of Baden-Powell. Baden-Powell knew that the Chinese Boy Scouts were working hard under the pressure of a strong neighbor and personally wrote a letter to commend and comfort them. Lytton was amazed by the excellence of the Chinese Boy Scouts, which exceeded his expectations, so naturally, he wanted to talk to the loyal and beloved Boy Scouts first. During this time, the enemy's Boy Scouts were also very active in Shanghai. At the end of April, they were summoned by the naval commander, commended, and given souvenirs. After our country's Boy Scouts have contributed so much to the country, it is unknown what the government and society have to say about them. Of course, the service of the Boy Scouts was never to seek others' praise.

Education Circles Initiate Organization

China Educational Film Association

Prominent figures in the education circles, such as Duan Xipeng, Yang Xingfo, Luo Jialun, and Guo Youshou, jointly initiated the organization of the China Educational Film Association. They held a discussion meeting in Beijing on the 11th of this month and have drafted the association's constitution. The content states that the association aims to study and utilize films to assist education, promote culture, and assist the development of the educational film industry. The association's duties include research and improvement of educational films, production matters, investigation and statistics, and promotional matters; cooperation with the film industry in the production of educational films; suggestions to film administrative agencies and handling of entrusted matters from film administrative agencies; collaboration with international educational film agencies; and other matters. The association is located in the capital and may establish branches in various locations. Anyone with specialized research in education, literature, art, and science, or with contributions and experience in film technology and the film industry, may become a member of the association through introduction procedures. The association is currently soliciting members and will convene a general meeting at a later date when a sufficient number of members have been obtained.

Three Departments Agree To

Transfer the Eastern Mausoleums to the Administration of the Beiping Cultural Institutions

The Executive Yuan, according to the request of Yi Peiji, the former director of the Palace Museum in Beiping, and others, to nationalize the forests of the Eastern Mausoleums and transfer them to the administration of the Beiping cultural institutions, was discussed by representatives of the three departments at a meeting at the Ministry of Industry. Those who attended the meeting at the Ministry of Industry yesterday morning included Shen Xihong, director of the Forestry and Reclamation Department of the Ministry of Industry, Technician Pi Zuoqiong, Luo Yaoshu, clerk of the Department of Rites and Customs of the Ministry of Interior, and Peng Baichuan, chief of the Social Affairs Department of the Ministry of Education. The result of the discussion was a resolution that (1) all mausoleum forests and their affiliated industries within the Eastern Mausoleums shall be nationalized; (2) the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Interior shall send representatives to jointly receive the forests with the Beiping Research Institute and propose measures for reorganization and preservation to be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval; (3) the three departments shall jointly submit the results of today's meeting to the Executive Yuan for instructions.
